<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошний</a> (8368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тамо</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tamo</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">there</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">támošnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> of that place, of those places, local
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тамошний.html>та́мошние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́тели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>támošnije</b> žíteli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the inhabitants there; the inhabitants of that place; locals</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:танковый.html>та́нковая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дивизия.html>диви́зия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tánkovaja</b> divízija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">armored division</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***танцевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:танцевать.html>танцева́ть</a> (2402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">танц-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tanc-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ева́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:танцевать.html>танцева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tancevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потанцевать.html>потанцева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dance (move rhythmically to music)</li></ol>

***таран.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́н</a> (16479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">taran</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">tarant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">siege machine, scorpion, dragon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">tarantola</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tarantula</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tarán</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battering ram</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval<span class="ib-comma">,</span> technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ram
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гидравли́ческий <a href = vnd.unilang:таран.html>тара́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gidravlíčeskij tarán</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hydraulic ram</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> battering ram attack</li></ol>

***тарахтеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тарахтеть.html>тарахте́ть</a> (18870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тараторить.html>тарато́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taratóritʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to chatter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарарам.html>тарара́м</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tararám</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">uproar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарахтеть.html>тарахте́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">taraxtétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rattle, to clatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chatter, to talk idly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chatter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тараторить.html>тарато́рить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taratóritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***тарелка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лка</a> (1945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">talerz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with metathesis (transposition) of <i>l</i> and <i>r</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tarélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plate <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a serving dish</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><i>(plural)</i> cymbals</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plate, disc
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:буфер.html>бу́фера</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tarélka</b> búfera</i> ― <span class="e-translation">buffer disc</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тариф.html>тари́ф</a> (10648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">tariffa</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">تَعْرِفَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taʿrifa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
